Topic: pizza ### Response: 

Question:
A pizzeria sells 100 pizzas on Monday. 200 more pizzas are sold on Tuesday. 100 pizzas are sold on Wednesday. 50 pizzas are returned. How many pizzas are sold at the end of Wednesday?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Pizzas sold on Monday
    pizzas_sold_monday = 100
    #Pizzas sold on Tuesday
    pizzas_sold_tuesday = 200
    #Pizzas sold on Wednesday
    pizzas_sold_wednesday = 100
    #Pizzas returned
    pizzas_returned = 50
    #The answer is
    result = pizzas_sold_monday + pizzas_sold_tuesday + pizzas_sold_wednesday - pizzas_returned
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The Warriors have 12 players. 3 of the players are point guards, 4 of the players are shooting guards, 3 of the players are small forwards, 1 of the players is a power forward, and 1 of the players is a center. How many players on the Warriors are not point guards, shooting guards, small forwards, power forwards, or centers?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #The number of point guards, shooting guards, small forwards, power forwards, and centers
    point_guards = 3
    shooting_guards = 4
    small_forwards = 3
    power_forwards = 1
    centers = 1
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - point_guards - shooting_guards - small_forwards - power_forwards - centers
    return result

    total_players = 25

    # players from Vancouver and Toronto

    players_from_vancouver = 10

    players_from_toronto = 7

    # players from Montreal

    players_from_montreal = total_players - players_from_vancouver - players_from_toronto

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 8 slices. 2 slices are eaten. 1/2 of the remaining slices are eaten. How many slices are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza is cut into 8 slices
    slices_initial = 8
    #2 slices are eaten
    slices_eaten_1 = 2
    #1/2 of the remaining slices are eaten
    slices_eaten_2 = (slices_initial - slices_eaten_1) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = slices_initial - slices_eaten_1 - slices_eaten_2
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 

3 of the players are 6' 1" tall. 

4 of the players are 6' 2" tall. 

5 of the players are 6' 3" tall. 

How tall, on average, is a player on the volleyball team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #3 of the players are 6' 1" tall
    players_6_1 = 3
    #4 of the players are 6' 2" tall
    players_6_2 = 4
    #5 of the players are 6' 3" tall
    players_6_3 = 5
    #The average height of a player is
    result = (players_6_1 * 6.1 + players_6_2 * 6.2 + players_6_3 * 6.3) / 12
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 

Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 3 of the players are setters, 4 of the players are middle blockers, and 2 of the players are outside hitters. 
How many of the players are liberos or opposites?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of setters, middle blockers, and outside hitters
    setters = 3
    middle_blockers = 4
    outside_hitters = 2
    #Number of liberos and opposites is the total minus the setters, middle blockers, and outside hitters
    liberos_and_opposites = total_players - setters - middle_blockers - outside_hitters
    return liberos_and_opposites
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles. 14 of them are in singles, 13 are in women's doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many of them are in mixed doubles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles_total = 24
    #14 of them are in singles
    grand_slam_titles_singles = 14
    #13 are in women's doubles
    grand_slam_titles_doubles = 13
    #The rest are in mixed doubles
    grand_slam_titles_mixed = grand_slam_titles_total - grand_slam_titles_singles - grand_slam_titles_doubles
    #The answer is
    result = grand_slam_titles_mixed
    return result

    ryo_initial = 1000
    #He spends 500 ryo on ramen
    ryo_ramen = 500
    #He spends 2/5 of the remaining ryo on a new headband

    result = ryo_initial - ryo_ramen - ryo_headband
    return result

Topic: Batman ### Response: 
Question: Batman's utility belt has 10 pouches. He has 4 batarangs in each pouch. He has 5 grappling guns in 2 pouches. How many batarangs and grappling guns does he have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman has 10 pouches
    pouches = 10
    #He has 4 batarangs in each pouch
    batarangs_per_pouch = 4
    #He has 5 grappling guns in 2 pouches
    grappling_guns_per_pouch = 5
    #The answer is
    result = pouches * batarangs_per_pouch + 2 * grappling_guns_per_pouch
    return result

Question: Captain Marvel has 12 Infinity Stones. She has to give 3 of them to Thor and 4 of them to Iron Man. How many Infinity Stones does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel started with 12 Infinity Stones
    infinity_stones_initial = 12
    #She gave 3 to Thor
    infinity_stones_given_to_thor = 3
    #She gave 4 to Iron Man
    infinity_stones_given_to_iron_man = 4
    #The answer is
    result = infinity_stones_initial - infinity_stones_given_to_thor - infinity_stones_given_to_iron_man
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: 
The cheer leading squad has 2000 pom poms. 1000 are red, 500 are blue, 300 are yellow, and the rest are green. How many pom poms are green?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The cheer leading squad has 2000 pom poms
    total_poms = 2000
    #1000 are red
    red_poms = 1000
    #500 are blue
    blue_poms = 500
    #300 are yellow
    yellow_poms = 300
    #The rest are green
    green_poms = total_poms - red_poms - blue_poms - yellow_poms
    return green_poms

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor can hammer 2000 times in 20 seconds.  How many hammers can he do in 10 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor can hammer 2000 times in 20 seconds
    hammers_per_20_seconds = 2000
    #10 minutes is 600 seconds
    seconds_in_10_minutes = 600
    #The answer is
    result = (hammers_per_20_seconds / 20) * seconds_in_10_minutes
    return result

Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 

Question:

Ash Ketchum has 600 Poké Balls. 300 of them are for capturing Pokémon. 100 of them are for healing his Pokémon. 200 of them are for powering up his Pokémon. How many Poké Balls does he have left?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Ash Ketchum has 600 Poké Balls
    pokemon_pokes = 600
    #300 of them are for capturing Pokémon
    pokemon_capture = 300
    #100 of them are for healing his Pokémon
    pokemon_heal = 100
    #200 of them are for powering up his Pokémon
    pokemon_power = 200
    #The answer is
    result = pokemon_pokes - pokemon_capture - pokemon_heal - pokemon_power
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 
Question: Hello Kitty is a 3-pound kitten. She ate 1/2 a pound of kibble and 1/4 a pound of wet food. How much does she weigh now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty's initial weight
    initial_weight = 3
    #She ate 1/2 a pound of kibble and 1/4 a pound of wet food
    kibble_weight = 0.5
    wet_food_weight = 0.25
    #The answer is
    result = initial_weight + kibble_weight + wet_food_weight
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: A soccer team has 11 players. 2 of the players are goalies. 3 of the players are defenders. 5 of the players are midfielders. How many players are forwards?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A soccer team has 11 players
    total_players = 11
    #2 of the players are goalies
    goalies = 2
    #3 of the players are defenders
    defenders = 3
    #5 of the players are midfielders
    midfielders = 5
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - goalies - defenders - midfielders
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: The cheer leading squad has 24 members. 12 of them are sophomores, 8 are juniors, and the rest are seniors. How many are seniors?

    total_players = 24
    #The number of sophomores
    sophomores = 12
    #The number of juniors
    juniors = 8
    #The rest are seniors. The answer is
    seniors = total_players - sophomores - juniors
    return seniors

    spider_webs_goblin = 20

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry, the 2-time MVP, has 2000 points, 500 rebounds, and 300 assists. 

How many more points does he have than rebounds and assists combined?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 2000 points
    points = 2000
    #He has 500 rebounds
    rebounds = 500
    #He has 300 assists
    assists = 300
    #The answer is
    result = points - (rebounds + assists)
    return result
Topic: cars ### Response:

    total_cars = 1000
    #200 of the cars in the parking lot are red
    red_cars = 200
    #1/3 of the red cars in the parking lot are also convertibles
    red_convertibles = red_cars / 3

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza has 16 slices. 4 of the slices are pepperoni. 5 of the slices are mushroom. 3 of the slices are both pepperoni and mushroom. How many slices are neither pepperoni nor mushroom?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza has 16 slices
    pizza_slices = 16
    #4 of the slices are pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = 4
    #5 of the slices are mushroom
    mushroom_slices = 5
    #3 of the slices are both pepperoni and mushroom
    both_slices = 3
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_slices - pepperoni_slices - mushroom_slices + both_slices
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel has 100000 Zenn-La credits. She spends 10000 credits on a new spaceship, and 1000 credits on each of 30 Kree-Skrull War comics. How many credits does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel started with 100000 credits
    credits_initial = 100000
    #She spent 10000 credits on a new spaceship
    credits_spent_spaceship = 10000
    #She spent 1000 credits on each of 30 Kree-Skrull War comics
    credits_spent_comics = 1000 * 30
    #The answer is
    result = credits_initial - credits_spent_spaceship - credits_spent_comics
    return result

    passing_yards = 3000
    #He has 1000 more rushing yards
    rushing_yards = 1000
    #He has 2000 more receiving yards

    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: A Minecraft world is 256 blocks wide, 256 blocks long, and 128 blocks high. 10% of the blocks are air, 30% are stone, 40% are dirt, and the rest are water. How many water blocks are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Minecraft world is 256 blocks wide, 256 blocks long, and 128 blocks high.
    total_blocks = 256 * 256 * 128
    #10% of the blocks are air
    air_blocks = 0.1 * total_blocks
    #30% are stone
    stone_blocks = 0.3 * total_blocks
    #40% are dirt
    dirt_blocks = 0.4 * total_blocks
    #The rest are water. The answer is
    water_blocks = total_blocks - air_blocks - stone_blocks - dirt_blocks
    return water_blocks

Question: Super Mario has 3000 coins. He spends 1000 coins on mushrooms, 500 on fire flowers, and 200 on 1-ups. How many coins does he have left?

    coins_initial = 3000
    #He spent 1000 on mushrooms
    coins_spent_mushrooms = 1000
    #500 on fire flowers
    coins_spent_fire_flowers = 500
    #and 200 on 1-ups
    coins_spent_1_ups = 200
    #The answer is
    result = coins_initial - coins_spent_mushrooms - coins_spent_fire_flowers - coins_spent_1_ups
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 1000 points. 200 of those points are from kills. 300 of those points are from aces. 200 of those points are from blocks. 100 of those points are from assists. How many of the points are from other plays?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 1000 points
    points_total = 1000
    #200 of those points are from kills
    points_kills = 200
    #300 of those points are from aces
    points_aces = 300
    #200 of those points are from blocks
    points_blocks = 200
    #100 of those points are from assists
    points_assists = 100
    #The answer is
    result = points_total - points_kills - points_aces - points_blocks - points_assists
    return result
Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 
Question: Ash has 50 Pokémon. Brock has 30 more Pokémon than Ash. Misty has 10 fewer Pokémon than Brock. How many Pokémon do they have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash has 50 Pokémon
    ash_pokemon = 50
    #Brock has 30 more Pokémon than Ash
    brock_pokemon = ash_pokemon + 30
    #Misty has 10 fewer Pokémon than Brock
    misty_pokemon = brock_pokemon - 10
    #The total number of Pokémon is
    total_pokemon = ash_pokemon + brock_pokemon + misty_pokemon
    return total_pokemon

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The Phoenix Suns have 20000 points. 10000 of them are 2-point shots. 5000 of them are 3-point shots. The rest are free-throws. How many free-throws do the Suns have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Phoenix Suns have 20000 points
    points = 20000
    #10000 of them are 2-point shots
    two_point_shots = 10000
    #5000 of them are 3-point shots
    three_point_shots = 5000
    #The rest are free-throws
    free_throws = points - two_point_shots - three_point_shots
    return free_throws
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 
Question: Hello Kitty is 10 years old. 
She is 2 years older than her sister. 
Her sister is 5 years younger than her brother. 
Her brother is 20 years old. 
How old is the average Hello Kitty family member?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty is 10 years old
    hello_kitty_age = 10
    #She is 2 years older than her sister
    sister_age = hello_kitty_age - 2
    #Her sister is 5 years younger than her brother
    brother_age = sister_age + 5
    #Her brother is 20 years old
    #The average age is
    average_age = (hello_kitty_age + sister_age + brother_age) / 3
    return average_age

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The 49ers have 1000 total yards. 300 of them are rushing yards. 200 of them are receiving yards. 100 of them are return yards. The rest are passing yards. How many passing yards do they have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total yards
    total_yards = 1000
    #Rushing yards
    rushing_yards = 300
    #Receiving yards
    receiving_yards = 200
    #Return yards
    return_yards = 100
    #Passing yards
    passing_yards = total_yards - rushing_yards - receiving_yards - return_yards
    return passing_yards

    #Serena Williams has 23 Grand Slam titles
    total_grand_slam_titles = 23
    #13 of them are in singles
    singles_grand_slam_titles = 13
    #4 of them are in mixed doubles
    mixed_doubles_grand_slam_titles = 4
    #The rest are in women's doubles. The answer is
    womens_doubles_grand_slam_titles = total_grand_slam_titles - singles_grand_slam_titles - mixed_doubles_grand_slam_titles
    return womens_doubles_grand_slam_titles
Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team has 50 players. 10 of the players are on the offense, 20 are on the defense, and the rest are on special teams. How many more players are on the offense than on special teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 50 players
    players = 50
    #10 of the players are on the offense
    offense = 10
    #20 are on the defense
    defense = 20
    #The rest are on special teams
    special_teams = players - offense - defense
    #The answer is
    result = offense - special_teams
    return result
Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: 
A Minecraft player has 3000 blocks. 
He uses 20% of them to build a house. 
He then uses 10% of the remaining to build a fence. 
How many blocks does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The player started with 3000 blocks
    blocks_initial = 3000
    #He used 20% of them to build a house
    blocks_used_house = 0.20 * blocks_initial
    #He then used 10% of the remaining to build a fence
    blocks_used_fence = 0.10 * (blocks_initial - blocks_used_house)
    #The answer is
    result = blocks_initial - blocks_used_house - blocks_used_fence
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 

Question: 

1000 cars are in the parking lot. 

200 of them are red. 

300 of them are blue. 

400 of them are green. 

500 of them are black. 

How many of them are not red, blue, green, or black?

Solution:

def solution():

  # total number of cars
  cars_total = 1000

  # number of red cars
  cars_red = 200

  # number of blue cars
  cars_blue = 300

  # number of green cars
  cars_green = 400

  # number of black cars
  cars_black = 500

  # number of cars that are not red, blue, green, or black
  cars_not_red_blue_green_black = cars_total - cars_red - cars_blue - cars_green - cars_black

  # return the answer
  return cars_not_red_blue

    #He uses 20 of them to stop a runaway train
    spider_webs_used_1 = 20
    #He uses 30 of them to catch 30 bad guys

Topic: Batman ### Response: 
Question: Batman has 100 batarangs. He uses 20 batarangs to fight 20 criminals. He then uses 1/3 of the batarangs he has left to fight 1/2 of the remaining criminals. How many batarangs does he have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman has 100 batarangs
    batarangs = 100
    #He uses 20 batarangs to fight 20 criminals
    batarangs_used = 20
    #He then uses 1/3 of the batarangs he has left to fight 1/2 of the remaining criminals
    batarangs_left = batarangs - batarangs_used
    batarangs_used_2 = batarangs_left / 3
    criminals_remaining = batarangs_used_2 * 2
    #The answer is
    result = batarangs_left - batarangs_used_2
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: 125 people lined up to buy ice cream. 75 of them bought a 3-scoop cone. 40 of them bought a 2-scoop cone. 10 of them bought a 1-scoop cone. How many scoops of ice cream were sold?

Solution:
def solution():
    #125 people lined up to buy ice cream
    total_people = 125
    #75 of them bought a 3-scoop cone
    three_scoop_cone = 75
    #40 of them bought a 2-scoop cone
    two_scoop_cone = 40
    #10 of them bought a 1-scoop cone
    one_scoop_cone = 10
    #The answer is
    result = three_scoop_cone*3 + two_scoop_cone*2 + one_scoop_cone*1
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry, the basketball player, is 6 feet 2 inches tall. 6 feet is the same as 72 inches. 1 inch is the same as 2.54 centimeters. How many centimeters tall is Steph Curry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry is 6 feet 2 inches tall
    #6 feet is the same as 72 inches
    #1 inch is the same as 2.54 centimeters
    #His height in inches is 6*12 + 2
    height_in_inches = 6*12 + 2
    #His height in centimeters is
    height_in_centimeters = height_in_inches * 2.54
    return height_in_centimeters

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 3 of the players are setters. 5 of the players are hitters. The rest of the players are blockers. How many blockers are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A volleyball team has 12 players
    players = 12
    #3 of the players are setters
    setters = 3
    #5 of the players are hitters
    hitters = 5
    #The rest of the players are blockers
    blockers = players - setters - hitters
    return blockers

    #1 of the players is 6' 8" tall
    players_6_8 = 1
    #The answer is
    result = (players_6_2 * 6' 2" + players_6_4 * 6' 4" + players_6_6 * 6'

    result = total_pokemon - pikachu - squirtle - charmander - bulbasaur
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 4 of the players are 6'2" tall, 3 of the players are 6'4" tall, and the rest of the players are 6'6" tall.  How tall, on average, is the volleyball team in inches?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Players who are 6'2"
    players_6_2 = 4
    #Players who are 6'4"
    players_6_4 = 3
    #Players who are 6'6"
    players_6_6 = total_players - players_6_2 - players_6_4
    #Average height in inches
    result = (players_6_2 * 74) + (players_6_4 * 76) + (players_6_6 * 78) / total_players
    return result

    players_total = 12
    #5 of them are forwards
    forwards = 5
    #4 of them are midfielders
    midfielders = 4
    #3 of them are defenders
    defenders = 3

    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: Patrick Mahomes has 5000 square feet of living space. 20% of that is a gym. 10% of that is an office. 30% of that is a theater. 40% of that is the house. How many square feet is the gym?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 5000 square feet of living space
    living_space = 5000
    #20% of that is a gym
    gym_percentage = 0.20
    #10% of that is an office
    office_percentage = 0.10
    #30% of that is a theater
    theater_percentage = 0.30
    #40% of that is the house
    house_percentage = 0.40
    #The gym is
    gym_space = living_space * gym_percentage
    #The answer is
    result = gym_space
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: A soccer team has 22 players. 11 of the players are on the field, and the rest are on the bench. 4 of the players on the bench are goalies.  How many non-goalie players are on the bench?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 22
    #Number of players on the field
    players_on_field = 11
    #Number of players on the bench
    players_on_bench = total_players - players_on_field
    #Number of goalies on the bench
    goalies_on_bench = 4
    #Number of non-goalie players on the bench
    non_goalie_players_on_bench = players_on_bench - goalies_on_bench
    #The answer is
    result = non_goalie_players_on_bench
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 10 unicorns are in a herd. 10 unicorns in the herd are white. 7 unicorns in the herd are pink. 4 unicorns in the herd are both white and pink. How many unicorns in the herd are neither white nor pink?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of unicorns
    total_unicorns = 10
    #Number of white unicorns
    white_unicorns = 10
    #Number of pink unicorns
    pink_unicorns = 7
    #Number of unicorns that are both white and pink
    both_unicorns = 4
    #Number of unicorns that are neither white nor pink is
    neither_unicorns = total_unicorns - white_unicorns - pink_unicorns + both_unicorns
    return neither_unicorns

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: Patrick Mahomes has 5000 yards. 2000 of them are rushing yards. 10% of the passing yards are interceptions. 400 more rushing yards are lost. How many total yards does Patrick Mahomes have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 5000 yards
    yards_initial = 5000
    #2000 of them are rushing yards
    rushing_yards = 2000
    #10% of the passing yards are interceptions
    interceptions = (yards_initial - rushing_yards) * 0.1
    #400 more rushing yards are lost
    rushing_yards_lost = 400
    #The answer is
    result = yards_initial - interceptions - rushing_yards_lost
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:

    #2 of the Power Rangers each lose 1 sword
    swords_lost = 2 * 1

    swords_gained = 1 * 2

Question: Steph Curry is a basketball player. He has 1000 3-point shots. 200 of them are from the left side of the court. 300 of them are from the right side of the court. 500 of them are from the top of the key. How many of his 3-point shots are from the corners?

def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 1000 3-point shots
    shots = 1000
    #200 of them are from the left side of the court
    left_shots = 200
    #300 of them are from the right side of the court
    right_shots = 300
    #500 of them are from the top of the key
    top_shots = 500
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex is 20 feet tall. 3 T-Rexes are in a field. 2 of the T-Rexes are 10 feet taller than the 3rd T-Rex. How tall is the 3rd T-Rex?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex is 20 feet tall
    t_rex_height = 20
    #3 T-Rexes are in a field
    t_rex_count = 3
    #2 of the T-Rexes are 10 feet taller than the 3rd T-Rex
    taller_t_rex_height = t_rex_height + 10
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_height * t_rex_count - 2 * taller_t_rex_height
    return result

    #He uses 10 spider webs to make 1 spider web cocoon

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The home team scored 100 points in the first half of the game. The away team scored 200. 20% of the home team's points and 30% of the away team's points were field goals. How many points were not field goals?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The home team scored 100 points in the first half of the game
    home_team_points = 100
    #The away team scored 200
    away_team_points = 200
    #20% of the home team's points and 30% of the away team's points were field goals
    home_team_field_goals = 0.20 * home_team_points
    away_team_field_goals = 0.30 * away_team_points
    #The answer is
    result = home_team_points + away_team_points - home_team_field_goals - away_team_field_goals
    return result

    villains = 30
    #He can web-up 3 villains at a time

    #The answer is

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: 10000 cars are in a parking lot. 2000 of the cars are red, 3000 are blue, and the rest are green.  How many are green?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10000 cars are in a parking lot
    cars_total = 10000
    #2000 of the cars are red
    cars_red = 2000
    #3000 are blue
    cars_blue = 3000
    #The answer is
    cars_green = cars_total - cars_red - cars_blue
    return cars_green
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A scoop of ice cream is 150 calories. A 3-scoop ice cream cone is 450 calories. A 4-scoop ice cream cone is 600 calories. How many calories is a 5-scoop ice cream cone?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A scoop of ice cream is 150 calories
    calories_per_scoop = 150
    #A 3-scoop ice cream cone is 450 calories
    calories_3_scoop = 450
    #A 4-scoop ice cream cone is 600 calories
    calories_4_scoop = 600
    #A 5-scoop ice cream cone is
    calories_5_scoop = 5 * calories_per_scoop
    return calories_5_scoop

Topic: ice cream ### Response:

    #30 of the scoops are vanilla

Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America can punch 200 times in 10 seconds. How many times can he punch in 30 seconds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America can punch 200 times in 10 seconds
    punches_10_seconds = 200

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: I have 100 pieces of candy. I ate 10. I then ate 20% of the remaining candy. How many pieces of candy do I have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Initial number of candy
    candy_initial = 100
    #Candy eaten
    candy_eaten_1 = 10
    #Remaining candy
    candy_remaining_1 = candy_initial - candy_eaten_1
    #Candy eaten as 20% of the remaining candy
    candy_eaten_2 = candy_remaining_1 * 0.20
    #Remaining candy
    candy_remaining_2 = candy_remaining_1 - candy_eaten_2
    #The answer is
    result = candy_remaining_2
    return result

    #4000 of his points are 2-pointers

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:

    points_initial = 1500
    #He gains 200 more points when he beats the boss
    points_gained = 200
    #He then spends 1000 points on a new mushroom
    points_spent = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = points_initial + points_gained - points_spent
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: A dog has 4 legs. 10 more dogs are added. 15 of the dogs are brown. How many of the dogs are not brown?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A dog has 4 legs
    legs_per_dog = 4
    #10 more dogs are added
    more_dogs = 10
    #15 of the dogs are brown
    brown_dogs = 15
    #The answer is
    result = (legs_per_dog + more_dogs) - brown_dogs
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel can punch 200 times in 10 minutes. How many times can she punch in 15 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    # Captain Marvel can punch 200 times in 10 minutes
    punches_10_minutes = 200
    # 15 minutes is 1.5 * 10 minutes
    minutes_15 = 1.5 * 10
    # She can punch the same number of times in 15 minutes as in 10 minutes
    punches_15_minutes = punches_10_minutes * 1.5
    return punches_15_minutes
Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 

Question: Spiderman can shoot 10 webs per minute. 1/3 of the webs are used to swing, 1/3 of the webs are used to stop bad guys, and 1/3 of the webs are used to help people. How many webs does Spiderman use to help people in 10 minutes?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can shoot 10 webs per minute
    webs_per_minute = 10
    #1/3 of the webs are used to swing
    webs_swing = webs_per_minute / 3
    #1/3 of the webs are used to stop bad guys
    webs_stop_bad_guys = webs_per_minute / 3
    #1/3 of the webs are used to help people
    webs_help_people = webs_per_minute / 3
    #The answer is
    result = webs_help_people * 10
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 1000 shots on goal. 1/3 of the shots on goal were goals. 1/2 of the goals were scored by the attack. 1/3 of the goals scored by the attack were scored by the first attack. How many goals did the first attack score?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A lacrosse team has 1000 shots on goal
    shots_on_goal = 1000
    #1/3 of the shots on goal were goals
    goals = shots_on_goal / 3
    #1/2 of the goals were scored by the attack
    attack_goals = goals / 2
    #1/3 of the goals scored by the attack were scored by the first attack
    first_attack_goals = attack_goals / 3
    #The answer is
    result = first_attack_goals
    return result
Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The Denver Broncos, the 2016 Super Bowl champions, have 53 players on their roster. 22 of the players are on offense. 25 of the players are on defense. 6 of the players are on special teams. How many of the players are not on a specific team?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The Denver Broncos have 53 players on their roster
    players_total = 53
    #22 of the players are on offense
    players_offense = 22
    #25 of the players are on defense
    players_defense = 25
    #6 of the players are on special teams
    players_special_teams = 6
    #The answer is
    result = players_total - players_offense - players_defense - players_special_teams
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 

Question:

A dog show has 1000 dogs. 

200 of the dogs are beagles, 

300 of the dogs are golden retrievers, 

and the rest are dachshunds. 

How many dachshunds are at the dog show?

Solution:

def solution():

    # total number of dogs

    dogs = 1000

    # number of beagles

    beagles = 200

    # number of golden retrievers

    golden_retrievers = 300

    # number of dachshunds

    dachshunds = dogs - beagles - golden_retrievers

    # the answer

    return dachshunds

    #Pizza slices that are pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = total_slices / 4

Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: Super Mario is on a quest to save the Mushroom Kingdom. He starts with 100 coins. He spends 20 coins to buy a mushroom. He then spends 10 coins to buy a fire flower. He spends 30 coins to buy a star. How many coins does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario started with 100 coins
    coins_initial = 100
    #He spent 20 coins to buy a mushroom
    coins_spent_mushroom = 20
    #He spent 10 coins to buy a fire flower
    coins_spent_fire_flower = 10
    #He spent 30 coins to buy a star
    coins_spent_star = 30
    #The answer is
    result = coins_initial - coins_spent_mushroom - coins_spent_fire_flower - coins_spent_star
    return result

    turtles_150 = 2

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A plane can carry 200 people. 1/3 of the passengers are in first class, 1/2 of the first class passengers are men. 1/4 of the men in first class are wearing hats. How many men in first class on the plane are not wearing hats?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A plane can carry 200 people
    total_passengers = 200
    #1/3 of the passengers are in first class
    first_class_passengers = total_passengers * 1/3
    #1/2 of the first class passengers are men
    first_class_men = first_class_passengers * 1/2
    #1/4 of the men in first class are wearing hats
    first_class_men_hats = first_class_men * 1/4
    #The answer is
    result = first_class_men - first_class_men_hats
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 12 players. 4 of the players are 15 years old, 5 of the players are 16, and 3 of the players are 17. How many years old is the average player on the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of players of each age
    players_15 = 4
    players_16 = 5
    players_17 = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (players_15 * 15 + players_16 * 16 + players_17 * 17) / total_players
    return result

    total_passing_yards = 1000
    #200 of them are rushing yards
    rushing_yards = 200
    #300 of them are in the 1st quarter

    #200 of them are in the 3rd quarter

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A 747 airplane can hold 400 passengers. 
A 777 airplane can hold 300 passengers. 
How many more 747 airplanes than 777 airplanes are needed to hold 20000 passengers?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 747 airplane can hold 400 passengers
    passengers_747 = 400
    #A 777 airplane can hold 300 passengers
    passengers_777 = 300
    #20000 passengers
    passengers_20000 = 20000
    #The answer is
    result = (passengers_20000 / passengers_747) - (passengers_20000 / passengers_777)
    return result

    leap_distance = 200
    #He leaps 100 feet, and then 50% as far
    leap_100_feet = 100
    leap_50_percent = leap_100_feet * 0.5

    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter has 300 galleons. 100 of them are in Gringotts, 100 of them are in vault 713, and the rest are in vault 687. How many galleons are in vault 687?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry Potter has 300 galleons
    galleons_total = 300
    #100 of them are in Gringotts
    galleons_gringotts = 100
    #100 of them are in vault 713
    galleons_vault_713 = 100
    #The rest are in vault 687
    galleons_vault_687 = galleons_total - galleons_gringotts - galleons_vault_713
    return galleons_vault_687

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter, Ron Weasley, and Hermione Granger each have 100 galleons. Ron Weasley has 20 more galleons than Hermione Granger. How many galleons does Harry Potter have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry Potter, Ron Weasley, and Hermione Granger each have 100 galleons
    galleons_initial = 100
    #Ron Weasley has 20 more galleons than Hermione Granger
    ron_galleons = galleons_initial + 20
    #The answer is
    result = galleons_initial - ron_galleons
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A 270-car freight train is 1.5 miles long.  How many miles long would a 540-car freight train be?  (Assume that all freight cars are the same length.)
Solution:
def solution():
    #1 freight car is 1.5 miles/270 cars = 0.00555556 miles long
    car_length = 1.5 / 270
    #540 cars
    num_cars = 540
    #The answer is
    result = car_length * num_cars
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex is 20 feet long. A Velociraptor is 1/4 the size of a T-Rex. A Stegosaurus is 2/3 the size of a T-Rex. How many feet long is a Velociraptor?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex is 20 feet long
    t_rex_size = 20
    #A Velociraptor is 1/4 the size of a T-Rex
    velociraptor_size = t_rex_size / 4
    #A Stegosaurus is 2/3 the size of a T-Rex
    stegosaurus_size = t_rex_size * 2/3
    #The answer is
    result = velociraptor_size
    return result

Solution:

    slices = 8
    #3 of the slices have pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 3
    #2 of the slices have mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 2
    #2 of the slices have peppers
    slices_peppers = 2
    #1 of the slices has onions
    slices_onions = 1
    #The answer is
    result = slices_pepperoni + slices_mushrooms + slices_peppers + slices_onions
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: 20 planes are at an airport. 10 more planes land at the airport. 5 of the planes that were at the airport when the 10 planes landed, take off. 2 of the planes that just landed, take off. How many planes are at the airport now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 planes are at an airport
    planes_initial = 20
    #10 more planes land at the airport
    planes_landed = 10
    #5 of the planes that were at the airport when the 10 planes landed, take off
    planes_took_off_1 = 5
    #2 of the planes that just landed, take off
    planes_took_off_2 = 2
    #The answer is
    result = planes_initial + planes_landed - planes_took_off_1 - planes_took_off_2
    return result

    players_total = 11
    #3 of the players are forwards
    forwards = 3
    #5 of the players are midfielders

    batarangs_initial = 100
    #He used 10 to fight the Riddler
    batarangs_riddler = 10
    #20 to fight the Penguin
    batarangs_penguin = 20
    #And 30 to fight the Joker

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A baker bakes 120 cakes. He sells 40 cakes on Monday and 30 cakes on Tuesday. 10 cakes are returned on Wednesday. How many cakes does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The baker started with 120 cakes
    cakes_initial = 120
    #He sold 40 on Monday and 30 on Tuesday
    cakes_sold_monday = 40
    cakes_sold_tuesday = 30
    #10 cakes were returned on Wednesday
    cakes_returned = 10
    #The answer is
    result = cakes_initial - cakes_sold_monday - cakes_sold_tuesday + cakes_returned
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: There are 5 Power Rangers. 2 of them are 15 years old, 2 of them are 17 years old, and 1 of them is 19. What is the average age of a Power Ranger?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2 of them are 15 years old
    rangers_15 = 2
    #2 of them are 17 years old
    rangers_17 = 2
    #1 of them is 19
    rangers_19 = 1
    #The answer is
    result = (rangers_15 * 15 + rangers_17 * 17 + rangers_19 * 19) / 5
    return result

### Instruction:
Write a grade school math word problem and Python function with a commented out step-by-step solution to solve the word problem.

### Response: Question: 100 Fortnite players were in a match. 20 more players joined. 40% of the players were eliminated. How many players are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 players were in a match
    players_initial = 100
    #20 more players joined
    players_joined = 20
    #40% of the players were eliminated
    players_eliminated = 0.40
    #The answer is
    result = players_initial + players_joined - (players_initial + players_joined) * players_eliminated
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 

Question: 

A volleyball team has 12 members. 

4 of them are setters, 

5 of them are hitters, 

and the rest are liberos. 

How many liberos are on the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    # total members
    total_members = 12
    # setters
    setters = 4
    # hitters
    hitters = 5
    # liberos
    liberos = total_members - setters - hitters
    return liberos
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 
Question: Hello Kitty has 22 pencils. She bought 5 pencils on Tuesday, 7 pencils on Wednesday, and 12 pencils on Thursday. How many pencils does she have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty started with 22 pencils
    pencils_initial = 22
    #She bought 5 pencils on Tuesday
    pencils_bought_tuesday = 5
    #7 pencils on Wednesday
    pencils_bought_wednesday = 7
    #and 12 pencils on Thursday
    pencils_bought_thursday = 12
    #The answer is
    result = pencils_initial + pencils_bought_tuesday + pencils_bought_wednesday + pencils_bought_thursday
    return result
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: A cheer leading squad has 20 members. 10 of them are in the 8th grade, 8 of them are in the 7th grade, and the rest are in the 6th grade. How many are in the 6th grade?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of members
    total_members = 20
    #Number of 8th graders
    eighth_graders = 10
    #Number of 7th graders
    seventh_graders = 8
    #The rest are in the 6th grade. The answer is
    sixth_graders = total_members - eighth_graders - seventh_graders
    return sixth_graders
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: An ice cream shop has 1000 scoops of ice cream. 100 of the scoops are vanilla. 200 of the scoops are chocolate. 300 of the scoops are strawberry. 400 of the scoops are pistachio. How many of the scoops are not one of the four flavors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The ice cream shop has 1000 scoops of ice cream
    scoops_total = 1000
    #100 of the scoops are vanilla
    scoops_vanilla = 100
    #200 of the scoops are chocolate
    scoops_chocolate = 200
    #300 of the scoops are strawberry
    scoops_strawberry = 300
    #400 of the scoops are pistachio
    scoops_pistachio = 4
Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor has 2000 hammers. 500 of them are Mjolnirs. 300 of them are Uru hammers. 100 of them are Stormbreaker hammers. The rest are Vajra hammers. How many Vajra hammers does he have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor has 2000 hammers
    total_hammers = 2000
    #500 of them are Mjolnirs
    mjolnir_hammers = 500
    #300 of them are Uru hammers
    uru_hammers = 300
    #100 of them are Stormbreaker hammers
    stormbreaker_hammers = 100
    #The rest are Vajra hammers
    vajra_hammers = total_hammers - mjolnir_hammers - uru_hammers - stormbreaker_hammers
    return vajra_hammers
Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: There are 200 cars in a parking lot. 100 of the cars are Hondas, 50 are Toyotas, and the rest are Fords. How many Fords are in the parking lot?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cars
    total_cars = 200
    #Honda cars
    honda_cars = 100
    #Toyota cars
    toyota_cars = 50
    #Ford cars
    ford_cars = total_cars - honda_cars - toyota_cars
    return ford_cars
Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 
Question: Wonder Woman can lasso 20 villains in 10 minutes. 10 more villains arrive. How many minutes will it take for her to lasso all the villains?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman can lasso 20 villains in 10 minutes
    villains_10_minutes = 20
    #10 more villains arrive
    additional_villains = 10
    #The answer is
    result = (villains_10_minutes + additional_villains) / villains_10_minutes * 10
    return result
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 

Question: The field hockey team has 100 sticks. 20 of the sticks are broken. 10 of the sticks are in the locker room. 5 of the sticks are in the equipment room. 15 of the sticks are in the gym. How many sticks are on the field?

Solution:

def solution():
    #The field hockey team has 100 sticks
    sticks_initial = 100
    #20 of the sticks are broken
    sticks_broken = 20
    #10 of the sticks are in the locker room
    sticks_locker_room = 10
    #5 of the sticks are in the equipment room
    sticks_equipment_room = 5
    #15 of the sticks are in the gym
    sticks_gym = 15
    #The answer is
    result = sticks_initial - sticks_broken - sticks_locker_room - sticks_equipment_room - sticks

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James has 10000 points. He scores 2000 points in the 2016-2017 season, 2500 points in the 2017-2018 season, and 3000 points in the 2018-2019 season. How many points does he have now?

Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James started with 10000 points
    points_initial = 10000
    #He scored 2000 points in the 2016-2017 season
    points_2016_2017 = 2000
    #He scored 2500 points in the 2017-2018 season
    points_2017_2018 = 2500
    #He scored 3000 points in the 2018-2019 season
    points_2018_2019 = 3
Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 

Question: The four Ninja Turtles are eating pizza. Leonardo ate 21 slices, Raphael ate 25 slices, Donatello ate 24 slices, and Michelangelo ate 23 slices. How many slices of pizza did the four Ninja Turtles eat in total?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Leonardo ate 21 slices
    leonardo_slices = 21
    #Raphael ate 25 slices
    raphael_slices = 25
    #Donatello ate 24 slices
    donatello_slices = 24
    #Michelangelo ate 23 slices
    michelangelo_slices = 23
    #The answer is
    result = leonardo_slices + raphael_slices + donatello_slices + michelangelo_slices
    return result
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: The cheerleading squad has 11 members. 5 of the members are in 10th grade. 4 of the members are in 11th grade. 2 of the members are in 12th grade. How many members of the squad are not in 12th grade?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total members
    total_members = 11
    #Members in 10th grade
    tenth_grade = 5
    #Members in 11th grade
    eleventh_grade = 4
    #Members in 12th grade
    twelfth_grade = 2
    #Members not in 12th grade
    not_twelfth_grade = total_members - twelfth_grade
    return not_twelfth_grade
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams is a professional tennis player. She has 23 Grand Slam titles. 
Venus Williams, her sister, has 7 Grand Slam titles. 
How many more Grand Slam titles does Serena have than Venus?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 23 Grand Slam titles
    serena_grand_slam_titles = 23
    #Venus Williams has 7 Grand Slam titles
    venus_grand_slam_titles = 7
    #The answer is
    result = serena_grand_slam_titles - venus_grand_slam_titles
    return result
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: The U.S. field hockey team has 15 players. 
The U.K. field hockey team has 12 players. 
How many more players does the U.S. team have than the U.K. team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The U.S. team has 15 players
    us_players = 15
    #The U.K. team has 12 players
    uk_players = 12
    #The answer is
    result = us_players - uk_players
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: 1200 cars are on a 2-mile long highway. 300 of them are in the left lane, 400 of them are in the right lane, and the rest are in the center lane. 200 of the cars in the center lane are going 10 mph. 100 of the cars in the left lane are going 20 mph. 100 of the cars in the right lane are going 30 mph. How many of the cars are going 40 mph?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1200 cars are on a 2-mile long highway
    cars_total = 1200
    #300 of them are in the left lane
    cars_left_lane = 300
    #400 of them are in the right lane
    cars_right_lane = 400
    #The rest are in the center lane
    cars_center_lane = cars_total - cars_left_lane - cars_right_lane
Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: A Minecraft player has 1000 points. 
They lose 200 points in the first level and 300 points in the second level. 
How many points do they have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The player has 1000 points
    points = 1000
    #They lose 200 points in the first level
    points_lost_first_level = 200
    #They lose 300 points in the second level
    points_lost_second_level = 300
    #The answer is
    result = points - points_lost_first_level - points_lost_second_level
    return result
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: There are 5 Power Rangers. 2 of them are Red, 1 of them is Blue, and the rest are Yellow. How many Power Rangers are Yellow?

Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 5 Power Rangers
    power_rangers = 5
    #2 of them are Red
    red_power_rangers = 2
    #1 of them is Blue
    blue_power_rangers = 1
    #The rest are Yellow
    yellow_power_rangers = power_rangers - red_power_rangers - blue_power_rangers
    #The answer is
    result = yellow_power_rangers
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: 
A 12-scoop sundae has 3 scoops of chocolate, 5 scoops of strawberry, and 4 scoops of vanilla. 
How many scoops of ice cream in the sundae are not chocolate?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 12-scoop sundae has 3 scoops of chocolate
    chocolate_scoops = 3
    #5 scoops of strawberry
    strawberry_scoops = 5
    #4 scoops of vanilla
    vanilla_scoops = 4
    #The answer is
    result = 12 - chocolate_scoops - strawberry_scoops - vanilla_scoops
    return result
Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A plane flies 1,200 miles in 4 hours. How many miles does the plane fly in 1 hour?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A plane flies 1,200 miles in 4 hours
    miles_4_hours = 1200
    #1 hour is 25% of 4 hours
    time_fraction = 1 / 4
    #The answer is
    result = miles_4_hours * time_fraction
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: I have 100 lollipops. I ate 20 of them. I gave 30 of them to my friends. How many lollipops do I have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #I started with 100 lollipops
    lollipops_initial = 100
    #I ate 20 of them
    lollipops_ate = 20
    #I gave 30 of them to my friends
    lollipops_friends = 30
    #The answer is
    result = lollipops_initial - lollipops_ate - lollipops_friends
    return result
Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 1000 micro-missiles. 300 of them are in his left arm, 400 of them are in his right arm, and the rest are in his legs. How many micro-missiles are in his legs?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 1000 micro-missiles
    micro_missiles = 1000
    #300 of them are in his left arm
    micro_missiles_left_arm = 300
    #400 of them are in his right arm
    micro_missiles_right_arm = 400
    #The rest are in his legs
    micro_missiles_legs = micro_missiles - micro_missiles_left_arm - micro_missiles_right_arm
    #The answer is
    result = micro_missiles_legs
    return result

    middle_cheerleaders = back_cheerleaders / 3
    #1/4 of the cheerleaders in the middle are in the front
    front_cheerleaders = middle_cheerleaders / 4
    #The answer is
    result = front_che

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A bakery baked 120 pies. They sold 40 pies in the morning, 30 pies in the afternoon, and 20 pies in the evening. How many pies do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The bakery baked 120 pies
    pies_baked = 120
    #They sold 40 in the morning, 30 in the afternoon, and 20 in the evening
    pies_sold_morning = 40
    pies_sold_afternoon = 30
    pies_sold_evening = 20
    #The answer is
    result = pies_baked - pies_sold_morning - pies_sold_afternoon - pies_sold_evening
    return result
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: The Power Rangers are a team of 5. 2 of them are the original rangers, and 3 of them are new. 1 of the original rangers and 2 of the new rangers are girls. How many boys are on the Power Rangers?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total Power Rangers
    total_rangers = 5
    #Original rangers
    original_rangers = 2
    #New rangers
    new_rangers = 3
    #Girls
    girls = 1 + 2
    #Boys
    boys = total_rangers - girls
    return boys
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 1200 shin guards.  They gave 200 to the B team and 300 to the C team.  How many shin guards does the A team have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The A team started with 1200 shin guards
    shin_guards_initial = 1200
    #They gave 200 to the B team
    shin_guards_given_b = 200
    #They gave 300 to the C team
    shin_guards_given_c = 300
    #The answer is
    result = shin_guards_initial - shin_guards_given_b - shin_guards_given_c
    return result
Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 

Question: LeBron James has 10000 points. He has 2000 more points than Steph Curry. How many points does Steph Curry have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James has 10000 points
    lebron_points = 10000
    #He has 2000 more points than Steph Curry
    steph_points = lebron_points - 2000
    #The answer is
    result = steph_points
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 3 of the players are setters. 4 of the players are middle blockers. 2 of the players are outside hitters. 1 of the players is a libero. 2 of the players are defensive specialists. How many players are not in a specialized position?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Setters
    setters = 3
    #Middle blockers
    middle_blockers = 4
    #Outside hitters
    outside_hitters = 2
    #Libero
    libero = 1
    #Defensive specialists
    defensive_specialists = 2
    #Players not in a specialized position
    result = total_players - setters - middle_blockers - outside_hitters - libero - defensive_specialists
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: The volleyball team at the University of Hawaii has 12 players. 8 of them are from Hawaii, 2 are from California, and the rest are from the mainland.  How many players are from the mainland?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 12 players
    players = 12
    #8 of them are from Hawaii
    hawaii_players = 8
    #2 are from California
    california_players = 2
    #The answer is
    result = players - hawaii_players - california_players
    return result
Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 
Question: A trainer has 500 Pokémon. 200 of the Pokémon are Pikachus. 100 of the Pokémon are Squirtles. 150 of the Pokémon are Charmanders. How many of the Pokémon are not Pikachus, Squirtles, or Charmanders?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A trainer has 500 Pokémon
    pokemon_total = 500
    #200 of the Pokémon are Pikachus
    pikachus = 200
    #100 of the Pokémon are Squirtles
    squirtles = 100
    #150 of the Pokémon are Charmanders
    charmanders = 150
    #The answer is
    result = pokemon_total - pikachus - squirtles - charmanders
    return result
Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Tony Stark has 35 Iron Man suits. 10 of the suits are in the lab, 14 of the suits are in the garage, and the rest are in the basement. How many suits are in the basement?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Tony Stark has 35 Iron Man suits
    suits_total = 35
    #10 of the suits are in the lab
    suits_lab = 10
    #14 of the suits are in the garage
    suits_garage = 14
    #The rest are in the basement
    suits_basement = suits_total - suits_lab - suits_garage
    return suits_basement

Iron Man is a superhero who flies with a jetpack.

He flies for 2 hours a day, 5 days a week. 
How many miles does he fly in a week?

Solution:

    #Iron Man flies at 1000 miles per hour
    speed = 1000
    #He flies for 2 hours a day
    hours_per_day = 2
    #5 days a week
    days_per_week = 5
    #The answer is
    result = speed * hours_per_day * days_per_week
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response:

    #He bakes 40 cookies on Monday
    cookies_baked_monday = 40
    #50 cookies on Tuesday

    #and 60 cookies on Wednesday
    cookies_baked_wednesday = 60
    #The answer is

Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: Michael Phelps swam 1000 meters in 4 minutes and 20 seconds. 2000 meters is an Olympic-sized swimming pool. How many Olympic-sized swimming pools can he swim in 1 hour?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael Phelps swam 1000 meters in 4 minutes and 20 seconds
    meters_swam = 1000
    time_swam = 4 * 60 + 20
    #2000 meters is an Olympic-sized swimming pool
    olympic_sized_pool = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = meters_swam / olympic_sized_pool * (60 * 60) / time_swam
    return result
Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: A dog has 4 legs. 20% of its legs are hurt. How many of its legs are not hurt?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A dog has 4 legs
    legs_total = 4
    #20% of its legs are hurt
    legs_hurt = 0.20 * legs_total
    #The answer is
    result = legs_total - legs_hurt
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: Michael Phelps swims 2000 meters per day. 200 of those meters are butterfly. 400 are backstroke. 600 are freestyle. 800 are breaststroke. How many meters of the 2000 is he not swimming one of the 4 strokes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael Phelps swims 2000 meters per day
    total_meters = 2000
    #200 of those meters are butterfly
    butterfly_meters = 200
    #400 are backstroke
    backstroke_meters = 400
    #600 are freestyle
    freestyle_meters = 600
    #800 are breaststroke
    breaststroke_meters = 800
    #The answer is
    result = total_meters - butterfly_meters - backstroke_meters - freestyle_meters - breaststroke_meters
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response:

    #3 of the players are setters

    #4 of the players are hitters

    #5 of the players are defenders

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza has 8 slices. 2 of the slices have pepperoni. 1 of the slices has mushrooms. 3 of the slices have pepperoni and mushrooms. 2 of the slices have just cheese. How many of the slices have mushrooms?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza has 8 slices
    pizza_slices = 8
    #2 of the slices have pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 2
    #1 of the slices has mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 1
    #3 of the slices have pepperoni and mushrooms
    slices_pepperoni_mushrooms = 3
    #2 of the slices have just cheese
    slices_cheese = 2
    #The answer is
    result = slices_mushrooms + slices_pepperoni_mushrooms
    return result
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: A cheer leading squad has 24 members. 12 of the members are on the stunt team, 8 of the members are on the tumbling team, and 4 of the members are on both the stunt and tumbling teams. How many members are on neither the stunt team nor the tumbling team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total members
    total_members = 24
    #Stunt team members
    stunt_team_members = 12
    #Tumbling team members
    tumbling_team_members = 8
    #Members on both the stunt and tumbling teams
    both_team_members = 4
    #Members on neither the stunt team nor the tumbling team
    neither_team_members = total_members - stunt_team_members - tumbling_team_members + both_team_members
    return neither_team_members

    #They won 4 of the 10 games by 10 points
    points_10 = 4
    #They won 3 of the 10 games by 14 points
    points_14 = 3
    #They won 2 of the 10 games by 7 points
    points_7 = 2
    #The answer is
    result = points_10 * 10 + points_14 * 14 + points_7 * 7
    return result

Question: Taylor Swift has 1000 cats. 200 of the cats are in the living room, 300 of the cats are in the kitchen, and 400 of the cats are in the bedroom. 

How many cats are not in the living room, kitchen, or bedroom?

    #200 of the cats are in the living room
    living_room_cats = 200
    #300 of the cats are in the kitchen

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The 49ers are up by 7 points in the 4th quarter.  They score a touchdown, but miss the extra point.  The 49ers' kicker then kicks a 30-yard field goal.  The 49ers' lead is now 10 points.  How many points is the other team down by?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The 49ers were up by 7 points
    points_49ers = 7
    #They score a touchdown, which is 6 points, and miss the extra point, which is 1 point
    points_touchdown = 6
    points_extra_point = 1
    #They kick a 30-yard field goal, which is 3 points
    points_field_goal = 3
    #The 49ers' lead is 10 points
    points_lead = 10
    #The answer is
    result = points_lead - (points_touchdown + points_extra_point + points_field_goal)
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: 100 cars are in a parking lot. 25 of them are red. 20 of them are blue. 30 of them are green. 15 of them are yellow. 10 of them are pink. How many of them are not red, blue, green, yellow, or pink?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cars
    total_cars = 100
    #Red cars
    red_cars = 25
    #Blue cars
    blue_cars = 20
    #Green cars
    green_cars = 30
    #Yellow cars
    yellow_cars = 15
    #Pink cars
    pink_cars = 10
    #The answer is
    result = total_cars - red_cars - blue_cars - green_cars - yellow_cars - pink_cars
    return result
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: In a field hockey game, each goalie can block 2 shots on goal. 10 shots on goal were made. How many goals were scored if there were 2 goalies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each goalie can block 2 shots
    shots_blocked_per_goalie = 2
    #There were 2 goalies
    num_goalies = 2
    #10 shots on goal were made
    shots_on_goal = 10
    #The answer is
    result = shots_on_goal - (shots_blocked_per_goalie * num_goalies)
    return result

    #The 2:00 train from Boston to New York is 30 minutes late
    boston_to_new_york_train_departure_time = 2 + 0.5
    #The trains pass each other in 3 hours

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
Question: Taylor Swift has 12000 Twitter followers. 20% of her followers are from the US, 40% are from the UK, and 10% are from Australia. The rest of her followers are from Canada. How many of her followers are from Canada?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift has 12000 Twitter followers
    followers_total = 12000
    #20% of her followers are from the US
    followers_us = followers_total * 0.2
    #40% are from the UK
    followers_uk = followers_total * 0.4
    #10% are from Australia
    followers_australia = followers_total * 0.1
    #The rest of her followers are from Canada. The answer is
    followers_canada = followers_total - followers_us - followers_uk - followers_australia
    return followers_canada

Solution:

    slices_total = 8
    #Number of slices with pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 3
    #Number of slices with mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 2
    #Number of slices with pepperoni and mushrooms
    slices_pepperoni_mushrooms = 1
    #Number of slices that are plain
    slices_plain = 2
    #The answer is
    result = slices_pepperoni + slices_mushrooms + slices_pepperoni_mushrooms
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is a superhero. She can punch 30 times per second. How many punches can she throw in 5 minutes?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel can punch 30 times per second
    punches_per_second = 30
    #There are 60 seconds in a minute
    seconds_per_minute = 60
    #5 minutes is 300 seconds
    minutes = 5
    seconds_in_5_minutes = minutes * seconds_per_minute
    #She can punch
    punches_in_5_minutes = punches_per_second * seconds_in_5_minutes
    #punches in 5 minutes. The answer is
    result = punches_in_5_minutes
    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter has 50 galleons. 10 galleons are in his vault at Gringotts. 20 galleons are in his piggy bank. 5 galleons are in his pockets. How many galleons does he have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry Potter has 50 galleons
    galleons = 50
    #10 galleons are in his vault at Gringotts
    galleons_in_vault = 10
    #20 galleons are in his piggy bank
    galleons_in_piggy_bank = 20
    #5 galleons are in his pockets
    galleons_in_pockets = 5
    #The answer is
    result = galleons - galleons_in_vault - galleons_in_piggy_bank - galleons_in_pockets
    return result
Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James is a basketball superstar. He has 550,000 Instagram followers. He has 200,000 more Twitter followers than he has Instagram followers. He has 100,000 more Facebook followers than he has Twitter followers. How many social media followers does LeBron James have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron has 550,000 Instagram followers
    instagram_followers = 550000
    #He has 200,000 more Twitter followers than he has Instagram followers
    twitter_followers = instagram_followers + 200000
    #He has 100,000 more Facebook followers than he has Twitter followers
    facebook_followers = twitter_followers + 100000
    #The answer is
    result = instagram_followers + twitter_followers + facebook_followers
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response: 

Question: Michael Phelps has 22 Olympic gold medals. 12 of them are for the 100m freestyle. 7 of them are for the 200m freestyle. 3 of them are for the 400m freestyle. How many of his gold medals are for other events?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael Phelps has 22 Olympic gold medals
    gold_medals_total = 22
    #12 of them are for the 100m freestyle
    gold_medals_100m_freestyle = 12
    #7 of them are for the 200m freestyle
    gold_medals_200m_freestyle = 7
    #3 of them are for the 400m freestyle
    gold_medals_400m_freestyle = 3
    #The answer is
    result = gold_medals_total - gold_medals_100m_freest

    strength_thor = 1000
    #A normal human can lift 100 pounds

    players = 11

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 12 players. 5 of them are in the starting lineup, and 2 of them are on the bench. How many players are not in the starting lineup or on the bench?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A volleyball team has 12 players
    total_players = 12
    #5 of them are in the starting lineup
    starting_lineup = 5
    #2 of them are on the bench
    bench = 2
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - starting_lineup - bench
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The San Francisco 49ers have 5000 rushing yards. The Dallas Cowboys have 1000 more rushing yards than the 49ers. The New York Giants have 2000 rushing yards. How many more rushing yards do the 49ers and the Giants have than the Cowboys?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The 49ers have 5000 rushing yards
    rushing_yards_49ers = 5000
    #The Cowboys have 1000 more rushing yards than the 49ers
    rushing_yards_Cowboys = rushing_yards_49ers + 1000
    #The Giants have 2000 rushing yards
    rushing_yards_Giants = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = rushing_yards_49ers + rushing_yards_Giants - rushing_yards_Cowboys
    return result

    #Cherry lollipops

    #Grape lollipops
    grape_lollipops = 1000
    #Strawberry lollipops
    strawberry_lollipops = 500

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 

Question: 

Wonder Woman can punch 1000 times in 10 seconds. 

1/4 of her punches are super punches. 

1/2 of her punches are uppercuts. 

1/3 of her punches are jabs. 

How many punches are neither super punches, uppercuts, nor jabs?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Wonder Woman can punch 1000 times in 10 seconds
    punches = 1000
    #1/4 of her punches are super punches
    super_punches = punches / 4
    #1/2 of her punches are uppercuts
    uppercuts = punches / 2
    #1/3 of her punches are jabs
    jabs = punches / 3
    #The answer is
    result = punches - super_punches - uppercuts - jabs
    return result
Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 100 unicorns are in a field. 20 of them are pink. 30 of them are purple. 50 of them are blue. How many unicorns in the field are not pink, purple, or blue?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total unicorns in the field
    total_unicorns = 100
    #Pink unicorns
    pink_unicorns = 20
    #Purple unicorns
    purple_unicorns = 30
    #Blue unicorns
    blue_unicorns = 50
    #The answer is
    result = total_unicorns - pink_unicorns - purple_unicorns - blue_unicorns
    return result
Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The Chicago Bears have 375 rushing yards and 250 passing yards. 200 of the rushing yards and 100 of the passing yards were in the first half. How many yards did they have in the second half?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Bears have 375 rushing yards and 250 passing yards.
    rushing_yards_total = 375
    passing_yards_total = 250
    #200 of the rushing yards and 100 of the passing yards were in the first half.
    rushing_yards_first_half = 200
    passing_yards_first_half = 100
    #The answer is
    result = (rushing_yards_total + passing_yards_total) - (rushing_yards_first_half + passing_yards_first_half)
    return result

    scoops_sold_per_day = 200
    #Each scoop sells for $2
    scoop_cost = 2
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_sold_per_day * scoop_cost
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza has 8 slices. 2 slices are pepperoni. 3 slices are mushroom. 1 slice is onion. 2 slices are plain. How many slices are not plain?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total slices in a pizza
    total_slices = 8
    #Slices with pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 2
    #Slices with mushroom
    slices_mushroom = 3
    #Slices with onion
    slices_onion = 1
    #Slices that are plain
    slices_plain = 2
    #Slices that are not plain
    slices_not_plain = total_slices - slices_pepperoni - slices_mushroom - slices_onion - slices_plain
    return slices_not_plain

Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: There are 1200 dogs in the city. 300 of them are in the west, 400 of them are in the east, 200 of them are in the north, and 100 of them are in the south. How many dogs are in the center?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of dogs
    total_dogs = 1200
    #Number of dogs in the west
    dogs_west = 300
    #Number of dogs in the east
    dogs_east = 400
    #Number of dogs in the north
    dogs_north = 200
    #Number of dogs in the south
    dogs_south = 100
    #The answer is
    result = total_dogs - dogs_west - dogs_east - dogs_north - dogs_south
    return result

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry, in a 10-game stretch, had 26, 28, 30, 32, 25, 20, 22, 24, 22, and 28 points.  What was his average points per game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph's points per game
    steph_points = [26, 28, 30, 32, 25, 20, 22, 24, 22, 28]
    #The answer is
    result = sum(steph_points) / len(steph_points)
    return result

    #100 of them are in the US
    planes_us = 100
    #50 of them are in Europe
    planes_europe = 50
    #20 of them are in Asia
    planes_asia = 20
    #The rest are in South America. The answer is
    planes_south_america = planes_initial - planes_us - planes_europe - planes_asia
    return planes_south_america

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is flying to a planet 200 light years away. She flies at 5000 miles per hour. How many hours will it take her to get there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A light year is 5,878,625,370,000 miles
    light_year = 5878625370000
    #200 light years is
    light_years = 200 * light_year
    #5000 miles per hour is
    miles_per_hour = 5000
    #The answer is
    result = light_years / miles_per_hour
    return result
Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman has 300 spider webs. He used 100 spider webs to save the day. He used 2/5 of the remaining spider webs to make a spider web cocoon. How many spider webs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman started with 300 spider webs
    spider_webs_initial = 300
    #He used 100 spider webs to save the day
    spider_webs_save_day = 100
    #He used 2/5 of the remaining spider webs to make a spider web cocoon
    spider_webs_cocoon = 2/5 * (spider_webs_initial - spider_webs_save_day)
    #The answer is
    result = spider_webs_initial - spider_webs_save_day - spider_webs_cocoon
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: 4000 planes were used in the D-Day invasion of Normandy. 2000 of the planes were fighters, 1500 were bombers, and the rest were transports. How many transports were there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of planes
    total_planes = 4000
    #Number of fighters
    fighters = 2000
    #Number of bombers
    bombers = 1500
    #Number of transports is the total number of planes minus the number of fighters and bombers
    transports = total_planes - fighters - bombers
    return transports

    total_players = 11
    #Players on offense
    offense_players = 3
    #Players on defense
    defense_players = 5
    #Players on special teams are the rest of the players
    special_teams_players = total_players - offense_players - defense_players
    return special_teams_players

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 10000 repulsor blasts. He used 2000 of them on the Hulk, 3000 of them on Thanos, and 1000 of them on Loki. How many repulsor blasts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man started with 10000 repulsor blasts
    repulsor_blasts_initial = 10000
    #He used 2000 on the Hulk
    repulsor_blasts_hulk = 2000
    #He used 3000 on Thanos
    repulsor_blasts_thanos = 3000
    #He used 1000 on Loki
    repulsor_blasts_loki = 1000

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 150 3-point shots
    three_point_shots = 150
    #30 of them are from the left corner
    left_corner_shots = 30
    #40 of them are from the right corner
    right_corner_shots = 40
    #30 of them are from the top of the key
    top_of_the_key_shots = 30
    #The rest are from the wing. The answer is
    wing_shots = three_point_shots - left_corner_shots - right_corner_shots - top_of_the_key_shots
    return
Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
def solution():

    #20 players are eliminated in the first 10 minutes

    #30 players are eliminated in the next 10 minutes
    players_eliminated_20_min = 30
    #40 players are eliminated in the next 10 minutes
    players_eliminated_30_min = 40
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 1000 repulsor blasts. He uses 200 of them to fight the Chitauri. He then uses 2/5 of what is left to fight the Dark Elves. How many repulsor blasts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man started with 1000 repulsor blasts
    repulsor_blasts_initial = 1000
    #He used 200 to fight the Chitauri
    repulsor_blasts_used_chitauri = 200
    #He used 2/5 of what is left to fight the Dark Elves
    repulsor_blasts_used_dark_elves = 2/5 * (repulsor_blasts_initial - repulsor_blasts_used_chitauri)
    #The answer is
    result = repulsor_blasts_initial - repulsor_blasts_used_chitauri - repulsor_blasts_used_dark_elves
    return result

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry has 2000 points. He scores 30 points per game. 
How many games does he have to play to get to 3000 points?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 2000 points
    points_initial = 2000
    #He scores 30 points per game
    points_per_game = 30
    #The answer is
    result = (3000 - points_initial) / points_per_game
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 1200 points. 20% of the points were from spikes. 30% of the points were from blocks. The rest of the points were from serves. How many points were from serves?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A volleyball team has 1200 points
    points_total = 1200
    #20% of the points were from spikes
    points_spikes = 0.20 * points_total
    #30% of the points were from blocks
    points_blocks = 0.30 * points_total
    #The rest of the points were from serves
    points_serves = points_total - points_spikes - points_blocks
    #The answer is
    result = points_serves
    return result

    #2 hours is 120 minutes

    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A 3-scoop ice cream cone has 1 more scoop than a 2-scoop ice cream cone. 
How many scoops of ice cream are in 10 3-scoop cones and 10 2-scoop cones?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 3-scoop cone has 1 more scoop than a 2-scoop cone
    scoops_3scoop = 3
    scoops_2scoop = 2
    #10 3-scoop cones have
    scoops_3scoop_cones = 10 * scoops_3scoop
    #10 2-scoop cones have
    scoops_2scoop_cones = 10 * scoops_2scoop
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_3scoop_cones + scoops_2scoop_cones
    return result

How many of the team's fans are not in the stadium and not wearing the team's jersey?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The soccer team has 1200 fans
    fans_total = 1200
    #400 of them are in the stadium
    fans_in_stadium = 400
    #200 of the fans in the stadium are wearing the team's jersey
    fans_in_stadium_wearing_jersey = 200
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: The field hockey team at the 1996 Summer Olympics had 11 players. 

- 2 of the players were from Australia
- 3 of the players were from New Zealand
- 5 of the players were from the United States
- 1 of the players was from the United Kingdom

How many players were not from these countries?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 11
    #Players from Australia, New Zealand, United States, and United Kingdom
    australia_players = 2
    new_zealand_players = 3
    united_states_players = 5
    united_kingdom_players = 1
    #Players from other countries
    other_countries_players = total_players - (australia_players + new_zealand_players + united_states_players + united_kingdom_players)
    return other_countries_players
Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: A unicorn ate 12 apples on Monday. It ate 23 apples on Tuesday. It ate 15 apples on Wednesday. It ate 14 apples on Thursday. How many apples did it eat in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The unicorn ate 12 apples on Monday
    apples_monday = 12
    #23 apples on Tuesday
    apples_tuesday = 23
    #15 apples on Wednesday
    apples_wednesday = 15
    #14 apples on Thursday
    apples_thursday = 14
    #The answer is
    result = apples_monday + apples_tuesday + apples_wednesday + apples_thursday
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 

Question: Steph Curry has 2400 points. He has 200 more 3-point shots than 2-point shots. He has 100 more free throws than 2-point shots. How many 2-point shots does he have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 2400 points
    total_points = 2400
    #He has 200 more 3-point shots than 2-point shots
    three_point_shots = 200
    #He has 100 more free throws than 2-point shots
    free_throws = 100
    #The answer is
    result = (total_points - (three_point_shots * 3) - (free_throws * 1)) / 2
    return result

### Response: Question: 3000 people are in line to buy the new Batman movie. 1000 of them are in the IMAX line. 2000 of them are in the 3D line. How many people are in the 2D line?
Solution:
def solution():
    #3000 people are in line to buy the new Batman movie
    people_total = 3000
    #1000 of them are in the IMAX line
    people_imax = 1000
    #2000 of them are in the 3D line
    people_3d = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = people_total - people_imax - people_3d
    return result

    pikachu_weight = 100
    #Squirtle is a 20-pound Water-type Pokémon.
    squirtle_weight = 20
    #Pikachu weighs 5 times as much as Squirtle.

    return result

    cookies_oatmeal_raisin = 200
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_total - cookies_chocolate_chip - cookies_peanut_butter - cookies_oatmeal_raisin
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: The lacrosse team has 10 players. The players use 3 sticks each. They are 40% out of sticks. How many sticks do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 10 players
    players = 10
    #Each player uses 3 sticks
    sticks_per_player = 3
    #They are 40% out of sticks
    sticks_left_percentage = 0.4
    #The total sticks is
    total_sticks = players * sticks_per_player
    #40% of that is
    sticks_used = total_sticks * 0.4
    #The answer is
    result = total_sticks - sticks_used
    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter is a wizard. He has 1000 galleons. 200 galleons is 1 knut. 10 knuts is 1 sickle. 29 sickles is 1 galleon. How many knuts does Harry Potter have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry Potter has 1000 galleons
    galleons = 1000
    #200 galleons is 1 knut
    galleons_per_knut = 200
    #10 knuts is 1 sickle
    knuts_per_sickle = 10
    #29 sickles is 1 galleon
    sickles_per_galleon = 29
    #The answer is
    result = galleons * galleons_per_knut * sickles_per_galleon * knuts_per_sickle
    return result

How many pom poms do they have left?
