    pom_poms_used_first_routine = 50
    #30 in the second routine
    pom_poms_used_second_routine = 30
    #and 20 in the third routine

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
Question: Taylor Swift is releasing 10 new songs. 5 of the songs are about her cats. 3 of the songs are about her ex-boyfriends. 2 of the songs are about her childhood. How many of the songs are about other topics?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift is releasing 10 new songs
    total_songs = 10
    #5 of the songs are about her cats
    cats_songs = 5
    #3 of the songs are about her ex-boyfriends
    ex_boyfriends_songs = 3
    #2 of the songs are about her childhood
    childhood_songs = 2
    #The answer is
    other_songs = total_songs - cats_songs - ex_boyfriends_songs - childhood_songs
    return other_songs
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 16 players. 8 of the players are from the US and the rest are from Canada. 3 of the Canadian players are from Toronto, and the rest are from Vancouver. How many players are from Vancouver?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 16 players
    total_players = 16
    #8 of them are from the US
    us_players = 8
    #The rest are from Canada
    canada_players = total_players - us_players
    #3 of the Canadian players are from Toronto
    toronto_players = 3
    #The rest are from Vancouver
    vancouver_players = canada_players - toronto_players
    #The answer is
    result = vancouver_players
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 1000 unicorns are at a unicorn convention. 300 unicorns left. 200 more unicorns showed up. How many unicorns are at the convention now?
Solution:
def solution():

    unicorns_initial = 1000
    #300 unicorns left
    unicorns_left = 300
    #200 more unicorns showed up
    unicorns_showed_up = 200

    result = unicorns_initial + unicorns_showed_up - unicorns_left
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: 
Patrick Mahomes is the best quarterback in the NFL. 
He has 1200 passing yards, 120 rushing yards, and 120 receiving yards. 
How many total yards does he have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 1200 passing yards
    passing_yards = 1200
    #120 rushing yards

Topic: Barbie ### Response: 
Question: Barbie has 1000 pink shoes. She gives 500 of them to her sister. She then gives 1/5 of the remaining shoes to her best friend. How many pink shoes does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie started with 1000 pink shoes
    pink_shoes_initial = 1000
    #She gave 500 of them to her sister
    pink_shoes_sister = 500
    #She then gave 1/5 of the remaining shoes to her best friend
    pink_shoes_best_friend = 1/5 * (pink_shoes_initial - pink_shoes_sister)
    #The answer is
    result = pink_shoes_initial - pink_shoes_sister - pink_shoes_best_friend
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 2000 balls. 1000 of the balls are blue and 1000 of the balls are red. 500 of the blue balls and 200 of the red balls are used in a game. How many balls are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team started with 2000 balls
    balls_initial = 2000
    #1000 of the balls are blue and 1000 of the balls are red
    balls_blue_initial = 1000
    balls_red_initial = 1000
    #500 of the blue balls and 200 of the red balls are used in a game
    balls_blue_used = 500
    balls_red_used = 200
    #The answer is
    result = (balls_initial - balls_blue_used - balls_red_used)
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: 
A field hockey team has 12 players. 

They are divided into 3 teams of 4 players each. 

Each of the 3 teams plays a match against the other 2 teams. 

How many matches are there in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    # there are 12 players in total
    total_players = 12

    # the players are divided into 3 teams of 4 players each
    teams = 3
    players_per_team = 4

    # each of the 3 teams plays a match against the other 2 teams
    # so each team plays 2 matches
    matches_per_team = 2

    # the total number of matches is the number of teams times the number of matches per team
    total_matches = teams * matches_per_team

    # the answer is
    result = total_matches
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A car can go 200 miles on 10 gallons of gas. How many miles can it go on 25 gallons of gas?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A car can go 200 miles on 10 gallons of gas
    miles_10_gallons = 200
    #It can go 250 miles on 12.5 gallons of gas
    miles_12_5_gallons = 250
    #It can go 300 miles on 15 gallons of gas
    miles_15_gallons = 300
    #The answer is
    result = (miles_15_gallons - miles_12_5_gallons) / (15 - 12.5) * 2.5
    return result

    gold_nuggets_pickaxe = 3000

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman has 200 spider webs. 100 of them are in the suburbs and 50 of them are in the city. The rest are in the forest. How many spider webs are in the forest?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman has 200 spider webs
    spider_webs_total = 200
    #100 of them are in the suburbs and 50 of them are in the city
    spider_webs_suburbs = 100
    spider_webs_city = 50
    #The rest are in the forest. The answer is
    spider_webs_forest = spider_webs_total - spider_webs_suburbs - spider_webs_city
    return spider_webs_forest

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: A cat has 20 toes. 10 of the toes are on the front paws and 10 of the toes are on the back paws. 2 of the toes on the front paws and 3 of the toes on the back paws are hurt. How many toes are not hurt?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A cat has 20 toes
    toes_total = 20
    #10 of the toes are on the front paws and 10 of the toes are on the back paws
    toes_front = 10
    toes_back = 10
    #2 of the toes on the front paws and 3 of the toes on the back paws are hurt
    toes_hurt_front = 2
    toes_hurt_back = 3
    #The answer is
    result = toes_total - toes_hurt_front - toes_hurt_back
    return result

    #He used 300 of them in a fight with Thanos
    repulsor_blasts_thanos = 300
    #And 200 of them in a fight with the Hulk

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: There are 120 lacrosse players. 50 of them are on the offense, 40 of them are on the defense, and the rest are on the sidelines. How many players are on the sidelines?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of lacrosse players
    total_players = 120
    #The number of players on offense
    offense = 50
    #The number of players on defense
    defense = 40
    #The number of players on the sidelines is
    sidelines = total_players - offense - defense
    return sidelines

How many hours will it take for him to get there?
Solution:

    #Wakanda is 2000 miles from the Bermuda Triangle
    wakanda_distance = 2000
    #Black Panther's top speed is 1,500 miles per hour
    black_panther_speed = 1500
    #The answer is

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team rushed for 150 yards, passed for 225 yards, and had 50 penalty yards. How many total yards did the team have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team rushed for 150 yards
    rushing_yards = 150
    #They passed for 225 yards
    passing_yards = 225
    #They had 50 penalty yards
    penalty_yards = 50
    #The answer is
    result = rushing_yards + passing_yards + penalty_yards
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: A cat has 3 kittens. 2 of the kittens are calico, 1 of the kittens is tabby. 1 of the calico kittens and the tabby kitten are female. 1 of the calico kittens is male. How many of the kittens are male?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A cat has 3 kittens
    kittens_total = 3
    #2 of the kittens are calico
    kittens_calico = 2
    #1 of the kittens is tabby
    kittens_tabby = 1
    #1 of the calico kittens and the tabby kitten are female
    kittens_female_calico_tabby = 2
    #1 of the calico kittens is male
    kittens_male_calico = 1
    #The answer is
    result = kittens_total - kittens_female_calico_tabby - kittens_male_calico

Question: Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles. 13 of the titles are in singles. 10 of the titles are in doubles. 4 of the titles are in both singles and doubles. How many of Serena Williams's titles are in doubles or both?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles
    titles_total = 24
    #13 of the titles are in singles
    titles_singles = 13
    #10 of the titles are in doubles
    titles_doubles = 10
    #4 of the titles are in both singles and doubles
    titles_both = 4
    #The answer is
    result = titles_doubles + titles_both
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question:
Patrick Mahomes has 400 touchdowns. 200 of them are in the first half. 300 of them are in the second half. 100 of the second half touchdowns are in the 4th quarter. How many touchdowns does Patrick Mahomes have in the 4th quarter of the first half?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 400 touchdowns
    total_touchdowns = 400
    #200 of them are in the first half
    first_half_touchdowns = 200
    #300 of them are in the second half
    second_half_touchdowns = 300
    #100 of the second half touchdowns are in the 4th quarter
    fourth_quarter_touchdowns = 100
    #The answer is
    result = first_half_touchdowns - fourth_quarter_touchdowns
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: The 12:00 train from New York to Boston is 30 minutes late. The 12:30 train from New York to Boston is 20 minutes late. How many minutes late is the 12:30 train to Boston compared to when the 12:00 train should have arrived?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The 12:00 train from New York to Boston is 30 minutes late
    train_1200_time = 12*60 + 30
    #The 12:30 train from New York to Boston is 20 minutes late
    train_1230_time = 12*60 + 30 + 20
    #The answer is
    result = train_1230_time - train_1200_time
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: The Stegosaurus is 100 feet long. The Apatosaurus is 20% longer than the Stegosaurus.  The T-Rex is 50% longer than the Apatosaurus.  How long is the T-Rex?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Stegosaurus is 100 feet long
    stegosaurus_length = 100
    #The Apatosaurus is 20% longer than the Stegosaurus
    apatosaurus_length = stegosaurus_length * 1.2
    #The T-Rex is 50% longer than the Apatosaurus
    t_rex_length = apatosaurus_length * 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_length
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: The Red Ranger, Blue Ranger, and Pink Ranger each have 12 Dino Gems. The Black Ranger and Yellow Ranger each have 14 Dino Gems. How many Dino Gems do the Power Rangers have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Red, Blue, and Pink Rangers each have 12 Dino Gems
    gems_red_blue_pink = 12
    #There are 3 of them
    num_red_blue_pink = 3
    #The Black and Yellow Rangers each have 14 Dino Gems
    gems_black_yellow = 14
    #There are 2 of them
    num_black_yellow = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (gems_red_blue_pink * num_red_blue_pink) + (gems_black_yellow * num_black_yellow)
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: A cat has 7 toes on each paw. 4 of its paws are in the front and the rest are in the back. How many toes does the cat have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A cat has 7 toes on each paw
    toes_per_paw = 7
    #4 of its paws are in the front and the rest are in the back
    paws_in_front = 4
    #The answer is
    toes_in_total = (toes_per_paw * paws_in_front) + (toes_per_paw * (paws_in_front + 1))
    return toes_in_total

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: There are 20 Power Rangers. 2 of them are Red Rangers, 4 of them are Blue Rangers, 7 of them are Pink Rangers, and the rest are Yellow Rangers. How many Yellow Rangers are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Power Rangers
    total_rangers = 20
    #Number of Red, Blue, and Pink Rangers
    red_rangers = 2
    blue_rangers = 4
    pink_rangers = 7
    #Number of Yellow Rangers is the total minus the Red, Blue, and Pink Rangers
    yellow_rangers = total_rangers - red_rangers - blue_rangers - pink_rangers
    return yellow_rangers

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team has 45 players. 20 of the players are on the offense. 15 of the players are on the defense. 10 of the players are on special teams. How many players are not on a team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A football team has 45 players.
    total_players = 45
    #20 of the players are on the offense.
    offense_players = 20
    #15 of the players are on the defense.
    defense_players = 15
    #10 of the players are on special teams.
    special_teams_players = 10
    #How many players are not on a team?
    result = total_players - offense_players - defense_players - special_teams_players
    return result
Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift has 1000 fans
    fans_initial = 1000
    #She is to give 200 autographs to each of the 5 cities she is to visit
    autographs_per_city = 200
    #There are 5 cities
    num_cities = 5
    #The autographs she gave away is
    autographs_given = autographs_per_city * num_cities
    #The fans she has left is
    fans_left = fans_initial - autographs_given
    #The answer is
    result = fans_left
    return result
Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman, the superhero, can shoot 10 webs per minute. 
He used 3 webs to catch a criminal, 5 webs to stop a speeding car, and 2 webs to save a kitten. 
How many webs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can shoot 10 webs per minute
    webs_per_minute = 10
    #He used 3 webs to catch a criminal, 5 webs to stop a speeding car, and 2 webs to save a kitten.
    webs_used = 3 + 5 + 2
    #The answer is
    result = webs_per_minute - webs_used
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 8 slices. 2 slices are left in the pizza box. 1 slice is in the refrigerator. 3 slices are in the trash. How many slices are eaten?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total slices in a pizza
    slices_total = 8
    #Slices left in the pizza box
    slices_left_box = 2
    #Slices in the refrigerator
    slices_refrigerator = 1
    #Slices in the trash
    slices_trash = 3
    #Slices eaten
    slices_eaten = slices_total - slices_left_box - slices_refrigerator - slices_trash
    return slices_eaten

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can fly 1000 miles in 1 hour. He flies 1000 miles from Metropolis to Gotham. He then flies 1000 miles from Gotham to Smallville. How many miles has he flown in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly 1000 miles in 1 hour
    miles_per_hour = 1000
    #He flies 1000 miles from Metropolis to Gotham
    miles_flown_1 = 1000
    #He then flies 1000 miles from Gotham to Smallville
    miles_flown_2 = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = miles_flown_1 + miles_flown_2
    return result
Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor has 1000 Mjolnirs.  He needs to fight 5000 Frost Giants.  Each Frost Giant is defeated with 2 Mjolnirs.  He still has 50% of his Mjolnirs left.  How many Frost Giants did he defeat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor has 1000 Mjolnirs
    mjolnirs = 1000
    #He needs to fight 5000 Frost Giants
    frost_giants = 5000
    #Each Frost Giant is defeated with 2 Mjolnirs
    mjolnirs_per_frost_giant = 2
    #He still has 50% of his Mjolnirs left
    mjolnirs_left = mjolnirs / 2
    #The answer is
    result = mjolnirs_left / mjolnirs_per_frost_giant
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 

Question:
Superman can fly at 1000 miles per hour. 
He flies from Metropolis to Gotham City. 
The distance between Metropolis and Gotham City is 2000 miles. 
How long does it take for Superman to fly from Metropolis to Gotham City?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Superman can fly at 1000 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 1000
    #The distance between Metropolis and Gotham City is 2000 miles
    distance = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = distance / superman_speed
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: A dog park has 200 dogs. 50 of the dogs are golden retrievers, 60 are labrador retrievers, and 20 are beagles.  How many dogs are not golden retrievers, labrador retrievers, or beagles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The dog park has 200 dogs
    total_dogs = 200
    #50 of the dogs are golden retrievers
    golden_retrievers = 50
    #60 are labrador retrievers
    labrador_retrievers = 60
    #20 are beagles
    beagles = 20
    #The answer is
    result = total_dogs - golden_retrievers - labrador_retrievers - beagles
    return result
Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman has 100 spider webs. He uses 20 spider webs to make a spider web cocoon. He uses 10 spider webs to make a spider web slingshot. How many spider webs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman started with 100 spider webs
    spider_webs_initial = 100
    #He used 20 spider webs to make a spider web cocoon
    spider_webs_cocoon = 20
    #He used 10 spider webs to make a spider web slingshot
    spider_webs_slingshot = 10
    #The answer is
    result = spider_webs_initial - spider_webs_cocoon - spider_webs_slingshot
    return result
Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question:
Steph Curry has 3000 points. He averages 30 points per game. He has 20 games left in the season. How many points will he have at the end of the season?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 3000 points
    points_initial = 3000
    #He averages 30 points per game
    points_per_game = 30
    #He has 20 games left in the season
    games_left = 20
    #The answer is
    result = points_initial + (points_per_game * games_left)
    return result
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: The Power Rangers are 5 teenagers with attitude. 1 of them is the Red Ranger, 1 of them is the Blue Ranger, 1 of them is the Pink Ranger, 1 of them is the Black Ranger, and 1 of them is the Yellow Ranger. How many Rangers are there of each color?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total Rangers
    total_rangers = 5
    #Red Ranger
    red_ranger = 1
    #Blue Ranger
    blue_ranger = 1
    #Pink Ranger
    pink_ranger = 1
    #Black Ranger
    black_ranger = 1
    #Yellow Ranger
    yellow_ranger = 1
    #The answer is
    result = (total_rangers - red_ranger - blue_ranger - pink_ranger - black_ranger) / 2
    return result
Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America has 100 vibranium shields. 25 of them are in his vault in Wakanda. 50 of them are in his vault in the Avengers Compound. The rest are in his vault in S.H.I.E.L.D. HQ. How many shields are in S.H.I.E.L.D. HQ?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America has 100 vibranium shields
    shields_total = 100
    #25 of them are in his vault in Wakanda
    shields_wakanda = 25
    #50 of them are in his vault in the Avengers Compound
    shields_avengers_compound = 50
    #The rest are in his vault in S.H.I.E.L.D. HQ. The answer is
    shields_shield_hq = shields_total - shields_wakanda - shields_avengers_compound
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: A cheer leading squad has 12 members. 3 of the members are also on the soccer team, 2 of the members are also on the track team, and 1 of the members is on both the soccer and track teams.  How many members of the cheer leading squad are not on either the soccer or track team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cheer leading squad members
    total_squad_members = 12
    #Number of members on the soccer team
    soccer_team_members = 3
    #Number of members on the track team
    track_team_members = 2
    #Number of members on both the soccer and track teams
    both_sports_members = 1
    #Number of members not on either the soccer or track teams
    not_on_either_sports_members = total_squad_members - soccer_team_members - track_team_members - both_sports_members
    return not_on_either_sports_members
Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can leap 1000 feet in a single bound. 
How far can he leap in 3 minutes if he leaps 1000 feet every 10 seconds? 
(1 minute is 60 seconds)

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can leap 1000 feet in a single bound
    leap_distance = 1000
    #He leaps 1000 feet every 10 seconds
    leap_rate = 1000 / 10
    #3 minutes is 180 seconds
    leap_time = 3 * 60
    #He can leap
    leaps = leap_time / 10
    #The answer is
    result = leap_distance * leaps
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: Michael Phelps swam 2000 meters in 10 minutes. He swam 1000 more meters in 5 minutes. 
How many meters per minute did he swim on average?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael Phelps swam 2000 meters in 10 minutes
    meters_10_minutes = 2000
    #He swam 1000 more meters in 5 minutes
    meters_5_minutes = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = (meters_10_minutes + meters_5_minutes) / (10 + 5)
    return result

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response:

    #1500 of them are on the road

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 20 Grand Slam titles. 10 of them are in singles, 7 of them are in women's doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many Grand Slam titles does she have in mixed doubles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 20 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 20
    #10 of them are in singles
    singles_titles = 10
    #7 of them are in women's doubles
    womens_doubles_titles = 7
    #The rest are in mixed doubles. The answer is
    mixed_doubles_titles = grand_slam_titles - singles_titles - womens_doubles_titles
    return mixed_doubles_titles

Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: A swimmer swam 100 laps. 20 of the laps were in the butterfly. 30 of the laps were in the backstroke. 40 of the laps were in the breaststroke. 10 of the laps were in the freestyle. How many of the laps were not in the freestyle?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A swimmer swam 100 laps
    total_laps = 100
    #20 of the laps were in the butterfly
    butterfly_laps = 20
    #30 of the laps were in the backstroke
    backstroke_laps = 30
    #40 of the laps were in the breaststroke
    breaststroke_laps = 40
    #10 of the laps were in the freestyle
    freestyle_laps = 10
    #The answer is
    result = total_laps - freestyle_laps
    return result

    #Pepperoni pizzas
    pepperoni_pizzas = 20

    mushroom_pizzas = 40
    #Onion pizzas
    onion_pizzas = 30
    #Pineapple pizzas
    pineapple_pizzas = 30
    #The answer is
    result = total_pizzas - pepperoni_pizzas
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 

Question: 

The Power Rangers have 100 Zords. 

The Red Ranger has 20 more Zords than the Blue Ranger. 

The Blue Ranger has 10 more Zords than the Pink Ranger. 

How many Zords does the Pink Ranger have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The Power Rangers have 100 Zords
    zords_total = 100
    #The Red Ranger has 20 more Zords than the Blue Ranger
    zords_red = zords_total + 20
    #The Blue Ranger has 10 more Zords than the Pink Ranger
    zords_blue = zords_total - 10
    #The Pink Ranger has
    zords_pink = zords_blue - 10
    return zords_pink

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 1000 aces. She aced 100 more in the first set, 150 more in the second set, and 200 more in the third set. How many aces does she have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams started with 1000 aces
    aces_initial = 1000
    #She aced 100 more in the first set, 150 more in the second set, and 200 more in the third set
    aces_first_set = 100
    aces_second_set = 150
    aces_third_set = 200
    #The answer is
    result = aces_initial + aces_first_set + aces_second_set + aces_third_set
    return result
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex is 20 feet long.  A Brontosaurus is 25% longer.  How long is a Brontosaurus?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex is 20 feet long
    t_rex_length = 20
    #A Brontosaurus is 25% longer
    brontosaurus_length = t_rex_length + (0.25 * t_rex_length)
    #The answer is
    result = brontosaurus_length
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: In Minecraft, a full stack of cobblestone is 64. 16 cobblestone is 1 stone. 4 stone is 1 smooth stone. 4 smooth stone is 1 smooth stone slab. 
How many cobblestone are in 12 smooth stone slabs?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A full stack of cobblestone is 64
    cobblestone_stack = 64
    #16 cobblestone is 1 stone
    cobblestone_to_stone = 16
    #4 stone is 1 smooth stone
    stone_to_smooth_stone = 4
    #4 smooth stone is 1 smooth stone slab
    smooth_stone_to_slab = 4
    #12 smooth stone slabs is
    smooth_stone_slabs = 12
    #The answer is
    result = smooth_stone_slabs * smooth_stone_to_slab * stone_to_smooth_stone * cobblestone_to_stone * cob

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 

Question: Serena Williams is a tennis player. She has 21 Grand Slam titles. 
Venus Williams, her sister, has 7 Grand Slam titles. 
How many more Grand Slam titles does Serena Williams have than her sister?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 21 Grand Slam titles
    serena_titles = 21
    #Venus Williams has 7 Grand Slam titles
    venus_titles = 7
    #The answer is
    result = serena_titles - venus_titles
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: A candy store has 200 lollipops. They sold 50 on Monday, 35 on Tuesday, and 45 on Wednesday. How many lollipops are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The candy store started with 200 lollipops
    lollipops_initial = 200
    #They sold 50 on Monday, 35 on Tuesday, and 45 on Wednesday
    lollipops_sold_monday = 50
    lollipops_sold_tuesday = 35
    lollipops_sold_wednesday = 45
    #The answer is
    result = lollipops_initial - lollipops_sold_monday - lollipops_sold_tuesday - lollipops_sold_wednesday
    return result

    #10 of the Poké Balls are for catching water-type Pokémon
    water_type_poke_balls = 10
    #20 of the Poké Balls are for catching fire-type Pokémon
    fire_type_poke_balls = 20

    grass_type_poke_balls = total_poke_balls - water_type_poke_balls - fire_type_poke_ball

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question:
Ice cream is $3.00 per scoop. 
How much would 100 scoops of ice cream cost?

Solution:
def solution():
  # define the price of a scoop of ice cream
  scoop_price = 3
  # define the number of scoops
  scoops = 100
  # calculate the total cost
  total_cost = scoop_price * scoops
  # return the total cost
  return total_cost

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: A Fortnite player has 10000 V-Bucks. They buy a 1500 V-Bucks outfit. They then buy a 2000 V-Bucks emote. How many V-Bucks do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The player started with 10000 V-Bucks
    vbucks_initial = 10000
    #They bought a 1500 V-Bucks outfit
    vbucks_outfit = 1500
    #They bought a 2000 V-Bucks emote
    vbucks_emote = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = vbucks_initial - vbucks_outfit - vbucks_emote
    return result
Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry made 15 3-point shots, 20 2-point shots, and 10 free throws. 
How many points did he score in the game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry made 15 3-point shots
    three_point_shots = 15
    #20 2-point shots
    two_point_shots = 20
    #and 10 free throws
    free_throws = 10
    #Each 3-point shot is worth 3 points, each 2-point shot is worth 2 points, and each free throw is worth 1 point.
    #The answer is
    result = three_point_shots * 3 + two_point_shots * 2 + free_throws * 1
    return result
Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 
Question: T'Challa, the Black Panther, is the king of Wakanda. 
Wakanda has 5 provinces. 
Each province has 3 tribes. 
Each tribe has 15 clans. 
How many clans are in Wakanda?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wakanda has 5 provinces
    provinces = 5
    #Each province has 3 tribes
    tribes_per_province = 3
    #Each tribe has 15 clans
    clans_per_tribe = 15
    #The answer is
    result = provinces * tribes_per_province * clans_per_tribe
    return result
Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: There are 100 cats in a cattery. 1/2 of the cats are in the cattery's outdoor play area. 1/3 of the cats in the outdoor play area have a toy. How many cats in the outdoor play area have a toy?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cats in the cattery
    total_cats = 100
    #1/2 of the cats are in the outdoor play area
    outdoor_cats = total_cats / 2
    #1/3 of the cats in the outdoor play area have a toy
    toy_cats = outdoor_cats / 3
    #The answer is
    result = toy_cats
    return result
